communal mindset walls are meant to protect groups and need many hands to build and staff it takes much less cooperation to build individual structures and arrange them so that the overlap provides mutual defense hence the angular semistreets also this world had been intermittently rediscovered by free traders and was a good market for what weapons the traders were willing to sell jump harnesses
